</aside></li></ul></div></nav><div class="site-inner"><div class="content-sidebar-wrap"><main class="content"><article class="post-49410 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-10-ingredients-or-less category-dairy-free category-egg-free category-fall category-gluten-free category-recipes category-refined-sugar-free category-soy-free category-spring category-summer category-sweet-things category-vegan category-vegetarian category-winter tag-almond-butter tag-avocado-oil tag-baking-powder tag-chocolate-chips tag-cocoa-powder tag-ice-cream tag-maple-syrup tag-oat-flour tag-pecans tag-sea-salt tag-sweet-potato tag-vanilla entry"><header class="entry-header"><h1 class="entry-title">Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)</h1>
</header><div class="entry-content"><div class="tasty-pins-hidden-image-container" style="display:none;"><img alt="Stack of Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies topped with a scoop of vegan vanilla ice cream" class="tasty-pins-hidden-image" data-pin-description="FUDGY Sweet Potato Brownies! 10 ingredients, SUPER rich, naturally sweetened! #sweetpotato #minimalistbaker #glutenfree #brownie #plantbased #recipe" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/MB-SweetPotatoBrownies-Pinterest.jpg" data-pin-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/MB-SweetPotatoBrownies-Pinterest-200x200.jpg"/></div>
<input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Stack of Sweet Potato Brownies topped with chocolate chips, pecans, and vanilla ice cream" class="wp-image-49340" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-17.jpg" data-pin-description="FUDGY Sweet Potato Brownies! <p>While attempting to create a more nutrient-rich brownie, we ended up creating our <strong>new <em>favorite</em></strong> <strong>brownie recipe</strong>! It’s happening.</p>
<p>Introducing super fudgy, naturally-sweetened, whole grain, <em>healthier</em> brownies made with just <strong>10 ingredients</strong>. Let’s bake!</p>
<iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/ND1A7B1Aug8" width="680"></iframe>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Coconut sugar, sweet potato, avocado oil, oat flour, and other ingredients for making our Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies recipe" class="wp-image-49344" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe.jpg" data-pin-description="FUDGY Sweet Potato Brownies! 10 ingredients, SUPER rich, naturally sweetened! #sweetpotato #minimalistbaker #glutenfree #brownie #plantbased #recipe" data-pin-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-217x300.jpg 217w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-768x1063.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-740x1024.jpg 740w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-600x830.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-680x941.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<span id="more-49410"></span>
<p>First, we make sweet potato purée by baking a sweet potato, removing the skin, and mashing in a bowl or <a aria-label="food processor (opens in a new tab)" href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Qt7mQg9Sth-GBdhOz4tCjhQAAAFurh6DCAEAAAFKAf_heOE/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00LBZOYAK/?creativeASIN=B00LBZOYAK&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=r1jIjjAnELfWUdjkwPJWEw&amp;slotNum=7&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">food processor</a>.</p>
<p>The sweet potato purée is then mixed with maple syrup, <a aria-label="almond butter (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/almond-butter-review/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">almond butter</a>, vanilla, and avocado oil.</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Using a wooden spoon to stir a bowl of Sweet Potato Brownie batter" class="wp-image-49331" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3.jpg" data-pin-description="FUDGY Sweet Potato Brownies! 10 ingredients, SUPER rich, naturally sweetened! #sweetpotato #minimalistbaker #glutenfree #brownie #plantbased #recipe" data-pin-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3-208x300.jpg 208w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3-768x1106.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3-711x1024.jpg 711w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3-600x864.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-3-680x979.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>Cocoa powder adds a rich, chocolatey flavor, oat flour keeps these whole grain and healthier than your average brownie, baking powder adds rise, and sea salt brings everything together.</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Using a wooden spoon to mix batter for making vegan Sweet Potato Brownies" class="wp-image-49335" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9.jpg" data-pin-description="FUDGY Sweet Potato Brownies! 10 ingredients, SUPER rich, naturally sweetened! #sweetpotato #minimalistbaker #glutenfree #brownie #plantbased #recipe" data-pin-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9-208x300.jpg 208w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9-768x1106.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9-711x1024.jpg 711w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9-600x864.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-9-680x979.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>Pecans and chocolate chips (optional) are added to the top for morsels of melty chocolate and a little toasty crunch with each bite. We highly recommend!</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Parchment-lined baking pan filled with a batch of Fudgy Gluten-Free Sweet Potato Brownies" class="wp-image-49336" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13.jpg" data-pin-description="FUDGY Sweet Potato Brownies! 10 ingredients, SUPER rich, naturally sweetened! #sweetpotato #minimalistbaker #glutenfree #brownie #plantbased #recipe" data-pin-title="Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13-211x300.jpg 211w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13-768x1090.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13-722x1024.jpg 722w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13-600x851.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/FUDGY-Sweet-Potato-Brownies-10-ingredients-SUPER-rich-naturally-sweetened-sweetpotato-minimalistbaker-glutenfree-brownie-plantbased-recipe-13-680x965.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>We hope you LOVE these brownies. They’re:<br/><br/>Fudgy<br/>Rich<br/>SUPER chocolatey<br/>Naturally sweet<br/>Healthier than your average brownie<br/>&amp; Incredibly delicious!</p>
<p>These brownies are delicious on their own but elevated with a scoop of vegan ice cream (<a aria-label="vanilla (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/vanilla-bean-coconut-ice-cream/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">vanilla</a>, <a aria-label="salted caramel (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/sea-salt-caramel-coconut-ice-cream/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">salted caramel</a>, and <a aria-label="coffee (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/coffee-coconut-ice-cream/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">coffee ice cream</a> would all be incredible).</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Fudgy Sweet Potato Brownies (V/GF)</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
<p>Incredibly fudgy sweet potato brownies with cacao, almond butter, and oats. Naturally sweetened with maple syrup and topped with pecans and chocolate chips for the ultimate healthier treat!</p> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-times-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-name">Prep Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time wprm-recipe-prep_time-minutes">50</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time-unit wprm-recipe-prep_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-name">Cook Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time wprm-recipe-cook_time-minutes">30</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time-unit wprm-recipe-cook_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-total-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-total-time-name">Total Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-hours wprm-recipe-total_time wprm-recipe-total_time-hours">1</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-unit-hours wprm-recipe-total_time-unit wprm-recipe-total_timeunit-hours">hour</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time wprm-recipe-total_time-minutes">20</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time-unit wprm-recipe-total_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>

<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="49500" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> – <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="49500" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">BROWNIES</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sweet potato purée</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(see instructions)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2/3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">maple syrup</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">almond butter or peanut butter</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">pure vanilla extract</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1 ½</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">avocado oil</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub melted vegan butter, melted coconut oil, or olive oil)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">cocoa powder or cacao powder </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(the higher quality the better // such as <a href="https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00B0CM3FC/?tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">this</a> one)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sea salt</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">baking powder</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2/3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-oat-flour/" target="_blank">oat flour</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(we also tested almond and coconut flour, and while they did work, we preferred oat // GF all purpose should also work)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chopped raw pecans (or sub walnuts, but we liked pecans better)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">dairy-free chocolate chips</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<em>optional</em>)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">FOR SERVING <em>optional</em></h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/vanilla-bean-coconut-ice-cream/" target="_blank">Vanilla Coconut Ice Cream</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(for store-bought, we prefer Luna and Larry's vanilla coconut ice cream)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/sea-salt-caramel-coconut-ice-cream/" target="_blank">Salted Caramel Coconut Ice Cream</a></span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/coffee-coconut-ice-cream/" target="_blank">Vegan Coffee Ice Cream</a></span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>To make sweet potato purée, halve sweet potato and brush the cut sides with oil (optional). Add to a parchment-lined baking sheet. Bake at 375 F (190 C) for ~25-30 minutes or until tender to the touch. Move to one side of pan and wrap the parchment paper over top to steam. Let steam for 5 minutes. Then peel away skin and mash in a mixing bowl (or <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Qu52uV8SUJEYI0jxFpa-s5gAAAFvZzoG3AEAAAFKAZryT0w/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00LBZOYAK/?creativeASIN=B00LBZOYAK&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=61WiyFGlXyc1VCIsr1K01A&amp;slotNum=5&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">food processor</a>). Set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Adjust oven temperature to 350 degrees F (176 C) and line an 8×8-inch baking pan (or similar-size pan) with parchment paper. Set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>To a large mixing bowl, add sweet potato purée, maple syrup, almond butter, vanilla extract, and avocado oil and stir to combine.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add cacao powder, sea salt, and baking powder and stir to combine. Then add oat flour and stir until a thick, scoopable batter is achieved (see photo).</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Transfer batter to your parchment-lined baking dish and spread into an even layer using a spoon or rubber spatula. Then top with pecans and chocolate chips (optional).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Bake on the center rack (at 350 F / 176 C) for 28-32 minutes. The brownie edges should appear slightly dry and a toothpick inserted into the center should come out mostly clean (a few crumbs are okay, but it shouldn’t be overly gooey). Remove from oven and let cool in the pan for 30 minutes – 1 hour.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Lift out of pan and slice. Enjoy warm or room temperature. Store leftovers covered at room temperature up to 3 days, in the refrigerator up to 5-7 days, or in the freezer up to 1 month. These brownies are delicious on their own but elevated with a scoop of dairy-free ice cream.</p></div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1" id="comment-864831">
<article id="article-comment-864831">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Anne" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/eb8ebabfcbd08883beabeda3748bef85?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/eb8ebabfcbd08883beabeda3748bef85?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Anne" width="96"><span itemprop="name">Anne</span> <span class="says">says</span> </img></p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-864831">February 20, 2020 at 7:32 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I’ve been looking for a whole foods brownie recipe that is delicious enough to withstand my swapping the cocoa out for carob (this lifetime chocoholic just got the bad news–no more chocolate.  Can you imagine?)  I decreased the maple syrup a bit and doubled the vanilla.  Even the batter was really, really good, and the finished product did not disappoint either! They hit all the right notes– rich, chewy, and utterly satisfying, even with carob.  The nuts and chips on the top are a brilliant touch.  Thank you for this inspired recipe.</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Annette Brown" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1eff45e3f21c6f2e48163960d90565d7?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1eff45e3f21c6f2e48163960d90565d7?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Annette Brown" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Annette Brown</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-863678">February 15, 2020 at 12:27 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I substituted the avocado oil out with applesauce, and used regular flour because store was out of oat flour.  Topped with pecans &amp; vegan dark chocolate chips, I shared this for Valentines with my 95 year old Mom, my son and my valentine, my husband.  I served it warm out of the oven with vanilla bean coconut ice cream! It was vegan and deliciously decadent! Oh and they baked perfectly, a little gooey, not a lot…this definitely fit the bill for a special Valentine dessert!</p>

<p>I LOVE this recipe. I have now made it using oat flour, and using regular flour. For the maple syrup I’ve used it as directed and once have to sub in Rosemary simple syrup bc it’s what I had and it worked great, and I’ve used peanut butter and also sun butter. I’ve put the chips and nuts on top and inside. All ways were delicious. I love this recipe I follow it exactly and sometimes I experiment with it a bit. But ALWAYS with the potato.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>OMG!<br>
Another amazing recipe. I baked these last night to send my boyfriend, who is working across the country, to include in a Valentine’s Day gift from home. I’m so glad I found this recipe. Ticks all the boxes… it’s vegan, it’s fudgy and indulgent, healthier than some other options, simple to make, and tastes phenomenal.<br>
Thank you for sharing this 5 star recipe.</br></br></p>

<img alt="Avatar for Eden" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/ed2cda975cd2cf3b1d21ba61caef68f5?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/ed2cda975cd2cf3b1d21ba61caef68f5?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Eden" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Eden</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-862115">February 10, 2020 at 11:28 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Delicious! The first time I made this it lasted less than 24 hours! </p>
<p>The second time I subbed date molasses for the maple syrup, which resulted in a slightly less sweet, denser version. I added a thin layer of stevia-sweetened chocolate ganache from your no-bake brownies. </p>
<p>I liked both versions, but I think the recipe as written is definitely more of a crowd pleaser.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-861521">
<article id="article-comment-861521">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Maria Misiura" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a53c4a1b81988f83399bd3c2e8af998b?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a53c4a1b81988f83399bd3c2e8af998b?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Maria Misiura" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Maria Misiura</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-861521">February 7, 2020 at 8:46 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>These are SUPER good, not too sweet or too rich, so very more-ish. Loved this recipe, and made a few modifications based on what I had available to me. I made these with a little less than a  1/2 cup of maple syrup and about 2 tbsp of xylitol. If using a solid sugar, I suggest adding an xtra tbsp of oil (I used coconut) to compensate for the liquid. I didn’t have oat flour so I used sprouted wheat flour and it worked perfectly! I also cooked the sweet potato in the microwave until it was really soft, and worked great. Note: because of the sweet potato it doesn’t have the texture of normal brownie batter, I kind of had to press it into the pan.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Jay, I appreciate the feedback! There are a lot of sweet potato brownie recipes out there and I can assure you we didn’t modify from that blog. Anytime we modify from someone else’s recipe we always give credit in the notes, if not also in the post. You’ll notice our ingredients and instructions are quite different from hers (for instance she adds a lot of sugar, and ours is sweetened with maple syrup).</p>
</div>

<p>These were just  incredible, thank you! (I like them better than the previous few I have tried here.) I want to also thank you for your recipes and enthusiasm- I am older, I think, than the majority of your fans and a really accomplished cook and baker. The coconut “bacon” was so addictive I ate it as a snack! Many thanks, Dana!</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-859082">
<article id="article-comment-859082">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Bridget" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/6fd12a0f6284b6cb43c7e6b2b79449cf?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/6fd12a0f6284b6cb43c7e6b2b79449cf?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Bridget" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Bridget</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-859082">January 31, 2020 at 8:30 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>These brownies are absolutely amazing! My dad and I made them last night. I’ve made sweet potato brownies in the past that weren’t as incredible so we were a little worried at first. These are truly some of the best brownies I’ve ever had! They’re fudgey, moist, chocolatey, and super rich. I can’t believe they’re made with better for you ingredients. </p>
<p>We peeled/cut the sweet potato into cubes and steamed them for 10-15 minutes until tender. Then we mashed them into a purée with a fork. We used cane sugar + 2 tbsp of water instead of maple syrup. For the oat flour, we blended 2/3 cup of rolled oats in a vitamix for 15 seconds. We used Trader Joe’s creamy salted almond butter as well. The brownies came out perfectly! They’re so unbelievably good. Thank you MB for another fantastic recipe!</p>

But will definitely make again with almond flour! (I’ve never see oat flour before)</br></p>

<p>This is an fantastic recipe. I made one batch as directed and a 2nd with half the amount of maple syrup and both turned out really well. This recipe is a keeper!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I was super surprised with how fudgy they actually are! It was the perfect evening treat that didn’t leave me feeling sluggish. For extra decadence, I topped it with some coconut whipped cream! It was delicious. I will most definitely make these again!</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-858400">
<article id="article-comment-858400">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Chloe" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fc9d4c3be131346d1cd6eda1a9dd815e?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fc9d4c3be131346d1cd6eda1a9dd815e?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Chloe" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Chloe</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-858400">January 29, 2020 at 8:15 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made these with the intention of taking the whole batch to my brother and sister-in-law the other day, but once I tasted a corner of the brownies, I realized it was going to be difficult to part with them! </p>
<p>They were so fudgy and rich-tasting (I didn’t have any almond butter and was too lazy to go and buy it, so I used tahini, which made the brownies taste like halvah. Not exactly complaining about that!), and tasted even better after being in a Ziploc bag overnight. Hard to believe that, as far as brownies go, these are pretty healthy.</p>
<p>These have unseated my previous favourite brownies (though I still love those!) and will definitely be going into my repertoire of treats!</p>
<p>And before anyone asks, yes, I did manage to spare a few for my brother and sister-in-law, who devoured half the bag in one sitting!</p>

I am already planning on making a double batch next weekend and (hopefully!) having some to put in my freezer.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt depth-3 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-858396">
<article id="article-comment-858396">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Juliana Boos" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e9c0437e4c9ea695eeab63c7c90de74c?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e9c0437e4c9ea695eeab63c7c90de74c?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Juliana Boos" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Juliana Boos</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-858396">January 29, 2020 at 7:30 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Tip when you’re measuring your sweet potatoes to bake: do more! I weighted around the amount needed, and after I baked it and peeled it, it was 70gr less than initially :(<br/>
I urgently cooked some in the microwave so I could go on with the recipe, and it turned out ok! :)</p>
<p>I substituted maple syrup for coconut syrup, and mixed pecans, hazelnuts and walnuts since I didn’t have enough pecans. I also sub chocolate chips for a bit less cacao nibs.</p>
<p>It turned out great, thank you! :)</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-857835">
<article id="article-comment-857835">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Jayden" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/f3b59b47331ef63478bf3131d2203b4b?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/f3b59b47331ef63478bf3131d2203b4b?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Jayden" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Jayden</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-857835">January 26, 2020 at 8:15 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Oh these are a dream! Tender, light. I’m in love with sweet potatoes so when I saw this in my inbox I had to make them right away, and I’m so so glad I did. This might be my new favorite brownie recipe ? ?</p>
<p>My batter was a bit thick (I used regular ap flour &amp; had mashed the yam with a whisk)– like, spoon-bending, patchy-flour thick– so I added a splash of almond milk and that helped the dries incorporate better. I only have an 8×6 pan so I baked at 345 for 35 mins, though next time I think I’ll go longer.</p>

<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Taylor" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e213dca98ef7bdc871f4dea1ccf3ef18?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/e213dca98ef7bdc871f4dea1ccf3ef18?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Taylor" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Taylor</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-857833">January 26, 2020 at 8:14 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This is one my favorite vegan brownie recipes! I used a GF flour blend instead of oat flour and 1/2 cup of maple syrup instead of the full 2/3 cup since we ran out. They were fudgy with a hint of cake texture. I also topped with chopped dark chocolate and almonds (we were out of pecans/walnuts). Your recipes never fail to impress!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>We’ve been gluten free for many years and vegan for 18 months. The entire time we’ve searched for a brownie recipe that also met my food restrictions (no soy or cashews, etc.). My husband has longed for a decent brownie during that time. We’ve tried so many things, and always been a bit disappointed until we tried this recipe. Thank you so much for such a rich, delicious brownie. We are so pleased that we think we can share this with our family members who are not GF/V and they will love it too. I love the healthy ingredients, too! Thank you.</p>
</div>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made these the other night. I did not have almond butter so I subbed for sunflower butter and omitted the vanilla, they are sweet enough with all the maple syrup. I found these needed longer than 30 mins in the oven but that could just be my oven. Ended up baking for almost 45m minutes.</p>
</div>

<article id="article-comment-857652">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Tara" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/5eb4c9ffd7249fc54562eec6e74aeed1?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/5eb4c9ffd7249fc54562eec6e74aeed1?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Tara" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Tara</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-857652">January 25, 2020 at 4:24 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>These are delish and kid approved! I have made them twice – the first time I reduced the sugar and only used 1/2 cup maple syrup because I knew I would be adding chocolate chips. They were still delish but better the second time when I made the recipe as written (go figure, lol!). They were not too sweet even with the full amount of syrup and chocolate chips. I find they keep and taste best when kept in the fridge because they are super fudgy. My kids and I both liked them best cool straight from the fridge. Delicious recipe I’ll be making again in the future!</p>

<p>Reduced the maple syrup to 1/2 cup and cooked for 28 min (they probs would have been good at 25 minutes), can out really nice!  Rich without being a sugar bomb.  I think this recipe would also work as an editable brownie dough.</p>

<p>I made these brownies and I must say… Delish!<br/>
I substituted cassava flour for oat flour and sunflower butter for the peanut butter. Lastly, I added cacao nibs as a garnish instead of chocolate chips. They turned out moist but more cakey than fudgy. Yum!</p>

<article id="article-comment-857413">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Gabrielle" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c5cbad9b986533ee2b1885ead36bd3d8?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c5cbad9b986533ee2b1885ead36bd3d8?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Gabrielle" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Gabrielle</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-857413">January 24, 2020 at 6:26 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Literally these brownies are so good. The second I saw the recipe on instagram I planned to make them that night! These are fudgey and rich brownies that have a nice crisp on the edges. I ended up having to cook them about 5 minutes longer than the recipe said. I am now going to keep steamed sweet potatoes on hand so I can make these whenever! Guiltless brownies!! Try them ASAP!</p>

<p>Oh my gosh! Divine! I made this for my children and their friends and they loved it.<br/>
I will make one change next time— I’m going to try to bake them in a mini muffin pan. They were pretty soft in the center I think mini muffins will be like mini vegan fondants.  Crispy on outside and a little gooey in inside</p>

<li class="comment odd alt depth-2 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-858173">
<article id="article-comment-858173">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Natty Nat" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/5470630b48c01931ba3e39ca837fcc6f?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/5470630b48c01931ba3e39ca837fcc6f?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Natty Nat" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Natty Nat</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411129#comment-858173">January 28, 2020 at 1:06 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I think you’re asking about the post-bake, pre-peel 5 minute steaming, right?  I did it on the cookie sheet I’d just taken out of the oven (folded the parchment paper over the potatoes), and they were perfectly easy to peel after 5 min as advertised!</p>
<p>These brownies were so amazingly yummy. I made 1.5x the recipe in a 9×13 pan, with 1/2 c. maple syrup and 1c. cocoa powder, and all the other ingredients at 1.5x the recipe quantities. So chocolatey and easily sweet enough with the decreased syrup.</p>
<p>Thanks Dana for this and so many other recipes that have become staples for my family. I’ve recommended your blog to many friends and relatives!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I’ve been making my own oat flour for some time now and always sub some in all sweet recipes.  It gives such a lovely texture and flavour.  As I’m gluten intolerant, everything I make is gluten free and adding oat flour to the gluten free flour makes it taste so much nicer.<br/>
Regards Nola</p>
</div>

<li class="comment odd alt depth-2 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-857692">
<article id="article-comment-857692">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Mattie" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a078fd6d1d3b2aa509740af50d369357?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a078fd6d1d3b2aa509740af50d369357?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Mattie" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Mattie</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411130#comment-857692">January 25, 2020 at 10:25 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made this brownie recipe with my chocoholic toddler son and husband in mind. I’m not a huge chocolate fan and the final result was tasty but overall too intensely chocolate for me and a bit bitter. I could taste the sweet potato (Barely) but not the almond butter (I used Barney butter)  in the finished product. </p>
<p>I had less maple syrup than I thought so I had to use some honey (since honey is sweeter I used about 25 percent less, and since it is thicker than maple syrup, I zapped it in the microwave first to get it similarly liquidy so it wouldn’t throw the texture off). I was out of oat flour so I had to make my own in the food processor which resulted in a slightly coarser grain than commercial oat flour but didn’t seem to skew the smooth texture of the finished product. </p>
<p>I doubled the recipe and used one 6 x 8 dish (32 minutes, center still a little gooey) and one 8 x 10 dish (40 minutes, haven’t cut into this batch yet). I found that I needed about two medium sweet potatoes to equal a full cup of purée, and since I only had two to start I had to cook another two in the microwave. </p>
<p>I really like the texture of the brownies and my son seemed to enjoy them. They are indeed rich and fudgy and Have a very concentrated chocolate Flavor. </p>
<p>I love Minimalist Baker and have made the banana bread, chocolate zucchini bread, pumpkin bread, and carrot cake over and over again. Thanks for putting gluten free, dairy free, vegan recipes out there!</p>

<article id="article-comment-857052">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Dana @ Minimalist Baker</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/fudgy-sweet-potato-brownies-v-gf/?t=1582411130#comment-857052">January 22, 2020 at 12:56 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>For best results we’d recommend our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/diy-gluten-free-flour-blend/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">GF blend</a>. Or you could try subbing all almond flour. We tested all coconut flour and didn’t love the texture, but in a pinch it’ll work (just use less as it’s quite absorbent).</p>
</div>

				// Used by Gallery Custom Links to handle tenacious Lightboxes
				jQuery(document).ready(function () {

					function mgclInit() {
						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.no-lightbox').click(mgclOnClick);

						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('a.set-target').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('a.set-target').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.set-target').click(mgclOnClick);
					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
